<p>The <b>2015–16 A-League</b> was the 39th season of top-flight soccer in Australia, and the 11th since the establishment of the <a href="/wiki/A-League" title="A-League">A-League</a> in 2004. <a href="/wiki/Melbourne_Victory_FC" title="Melbourne Victory FC">Melbourne Victory</a> were both the defending A-League Premiers and Champions. The regular season schedule was released on 29 June 2015. The season commenced on 8 October 2015 and concluded on 10 April 2016. The finals series commenced on 15 April 2016 and concluded with the 2016 Grand Final, held on 1 May 2016.</p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/2016_A-League_Grand_Final" title="2016 A-League Grand Final">2016 Grand Final</a> took place on 1 May 2016, with <a href="/wiki/Adelaide_United_FC" title="Adelaide United FC">Adelaide United</a> claiming their first Championship with a 3–1 win against <a href="/wiki/Western_Sydney_Wanderers_FC" title="Western Sydney Wanderers FC">Western Sydney Wanderers</a>.</p>

<p><small>The following do not fill a Visa position:<br/>
<sup>1</sup>Those players who were born and started their professional career abroad but have since gained Australian citizenship (and New Zealand citizenship, in the case of <a href="/wiki/Wellington_Phoenix_FC" title="Wellington Phoenix FC">Wellington Phoenix</a>);<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pfa-cba_10-0"><a href="#cite_note-pfa-cba-10">[10]</a></sup><br/>
<sup>2</sup>Australian citizens (and New Zealand citizens, in the case of <a href="/wiki/Wellington_Phoenix_FC" title="Wellington Phoenix FC">Wellington Phoenix</a>) who have chosen to represent another national team;<br/>
<sup>3</sup>Injury Replacement Players, or National Team Replacement Players;<br/>
<sup>4</sup>Guest Players (eligible to play a maximum of fourteen games);<br/>
<sup>5</sup>Signed only to <a href="/wiki/2016_AFC_Champions_League" title="2016 AFC Champions League">ACL</a> squad</small></p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Salary_cap_concessions">Salary cap concessions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2015%E2%80%9316_A-League&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Salary cap concessions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Introduced by the FFA for this season are the following concessions to the cap:<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42"><a href="#cite_note-42">[42]</a></sup></p>
<ol>
<li>A Loyalty allowance on a sliding scale for players who have played 5 years at the same club. Maximum $200,000 for 10 years.</li>
<li>A Mature Aged Rookie over the age of 21 who has not played in a fully professional league for the last 18 months and last played football in Australia.</li>
<li>Each Club can pay three players who started their careers with the club outside the Salary Cap. This season the total has been lifted from $150,000 to $200,000.</li>
<li>The two Marquee Players (which sit outside the Salary Cap) can be two foreigners.</li>
<li>Salary Cap Banking will allow clubs to carry over money not spent inside the Salary Cap in the previous two seasons to the following season, up to 105% of the Salary Cap in the relevant contract year.</li>
</ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Elimination-finals">Elimination-finals</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2015%E2%80%9316_A-League&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Elimination-finals">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="vevent"><span class="summary" style="display: none;"><a href="/wiki/Brisbane_Roar_FC" title="Brisbane Roar FC">Brisbane Roar</a> v <a href="/wiki/Melbourne_Victory_FC" title="Melbourne Victory FC">Melbourne Victory</a></span>

<td style="vertical-align:top" width="19%"><span style="white-space:nowrap;float:right;margin-left:.5em">15 April 2016</span></td>
<td class="vcard attendee" style="text-align:right;vertical-align:top" width="23%"><b><span class="fn org"><a href="/wiki/Brisbane_Roar_FC" title="Brisbane Roar FC">Brisbane Roar</a></span></b></td>
<td style="text-align:center;vertical-align:top" width="12%"><span style="white-space:nowrap; display:inline;"><b>2–1</b></span></td>
<td class="vcard attendee" style="vertical-align:top" width="23%"><b><span class="fn org"><a href="/wiki/Melbourne_Victory_FC" title="Melbourne Victory FC">Melbourne Victory</a></span></b></td>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Discipline">Discipline</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2015%E2%80%9316_A-League&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Discipline">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>During the season each club is given fair play points based on the amount of cards they received in games. A yellow card is worth 1 point, a second yellow card is worth 2 points, and a red card is worth 3 points. At the annual awards night, the club with the least amount of points wins the Fair Play Award.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50"><a href="#cite_note-50">[49]</a></sup></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="NAB_Young_Footballer_of_the_Year_Award">NAB Young Footballer of the Year Award</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2015%E2%80%9316_A-League&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: NAB Young Footballer of the Year Award">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/National_Australia_Bank" title="National Australia Bank">NAB</a> Young Footballer of the Year Award will be awarded to the finest U/23 player talent throughout the Hyundai A-League 2015–16 competition. One nominee is announced per month and all nominees will qualify to be named the NAB Young Footballer of the Year at the conclusion of the season.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Nominees">Nominees</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2015%E2%80%9316_A-League&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Nominees">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="End_of_season_awards">End of season awards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2015%E2%80%9316_A-League&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: End of season awards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The following end of the season awards were announced at the 2015–16 Dolan Warren Awards night held at the <a href="/wiki/Carriageworks" title="Carriageworks">Carriageworks</a> in Sydney on 26 April 2016.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-57"><a href="#cite_note-57">[56]</a></sup></p>
<ul>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Johnny_Warren_Medal" title="Johnny Warren Medal">Johnny Warren Medal</a></b> – <a href="/wiki/Diego_Castro" title="Diego Castro">Diego Castro</a>, <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;">Perth Glory !</span><span class="sorttext"><a href="/wiki/Perth_Glory_FC" title="Perth Glory FC">Perth Glory</a></span></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/A-League_Young_Footballer_of_the_Year" title="A-League Young Footballer of the Year">NAB Young Footballer of the Year</a></b> – <a href="/wiki/Jamie_Maclaren" title="Jamie Maclaren">Jamie Maclaren</a>, <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;">Brisbane Roar !</span><span class="sorttext"><a href="/wiki/Brisbane_Roar_FC" title="Brisbane Roar FC">Brisbane Roar</a></span></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/A-League_Golden_Boot" title="A-League Golden Boot">Nike Golden Boot Award</a></b> – <a href="/wiki/Bruno_Fornaroli" title="Bruno Fornaroli">Bruno Fornaroli</a>, <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;">Melbourne City !</span><span class="sorttext"><a href="/wiki/Melbourne_City_FC" title="Melbourne City FC">Melbourne City</a></span> (23 goals)</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/A-League_Goalkeeper_of_the_Year" title="A-League Goalkeeper of the Year">Goalkeeper of the Year</a></b> – <a href="/wiki/Thomas_S%C3%B8rensen" title="Thomas Sørensen">Thomas Sørensen</a>, <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;">Melbourne City !</span><span class="sorttext"><a href="/wiki/Melbourne_City_FC" title="Melbourne City FC">Melbourne City</a></span></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/List_of_A-League_honours#Coach_of_the_Year" title="List of A-League honours">Coach of the Year</a></b> – <a href="/wiki/Guillermo_Amor" title="Guillermo Amor">Guillermo Amor</a>, <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;">Adelaide United !</span><span class="sorttext"><a href="/wiki/Adelaide_United_FC" title="Adelaide United FC">Adelaide United</a></span></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/List_of_A-League_honours#Fair_Play_Award" title="List of A-League honours">Fair Play Award</a></b> – <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;">Brisbane Roar !</span><span class="sorttext"><a href="/wiki/Brisbane_Roar_FC" title="Brisbane Roar FC">Brisbane Roar</a></span></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/List_of_A-League_honours#Referee_of_the_Year" title="List of A-League honours">Referee of the Year</a></b> – <a href="/wiki/Jarred_Gillett" title="Jarred Gillett">Jarred Gillett</a></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/List_of_A-League_honours#Goal_of_the_Year" title="List of A-League honours">Goal of the Year</a></b> – <a href="/wiki/Roy_O%27Donovan" title="Roy O'Donovan">Roy O'Donovan</a>, <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;">Central Coast Mariners !</span><span class="sorttext"><a href="/wiki/Central_Coast_Mariners_FC" title="Central Coast Mariners FC">Central Coast Mariners</a></span> (<span class="sortkey" style="display:none;">Adelaide United !</span><span class="sorttext"><a href="/wiki/Adelaide_United_FC" title="Adelaide United FC">Adelaide United</a></span> v <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;">Central Coast Mariners !</span><span class="sorttext"><a href="/wiki/Central_Coast_Mariners_FC" title="Central Coast Mariners FC">Central Coast Mariners</a></span>, 27 March 2016)</li>
</ul>
